posted:Posted October 6, 2023
msg:Excellently located next to Chengdu East Railway station, by the East Square, the Longemont is a beautiful place to stay and brings a cleverly designed European flavour to the otherwise local Chinese culture on this side of town. Rooms are decorated in a simple but ornate style, and features such as the glass divide and sliding doorway in the bathroom, give a homely, stylish vibe to the place. All accessories and provisions are top quality here. The Skyline Bar on the 42nd floor gives an amazing view out over the city and the chef serves a full menu right up to midnight. There was also a great variety of food to choose from at breakfast, though if you tend to prefer coffee over tea, I would definitely recommend the lounge cafe on the ground floor, for the most carefully prepared espresso I‚Äôve tasted this side of Europe! There is a very convenient, securely managed luggage store in the front lobby, which is perfect for an early check-out if you want to explore and come back later to catch an evening train. Staff are warm, friendly and approachable. I appreciated the ease with which they would respond to any request without allowing intrusion. This has been another wonderful stay on my adventures, I will be back again next time I visit Chengdu.
